###################################################################
# Triggered modifiers are here.
# these are checked for each countries once/month and then applied.
#
# Effects are fully scriptable here.
###################################################################

minimal_training_active_I = {
	potential = {
		check_variable = {
			which = "minimal_training_days_active"
			value = 1
		}
		not = {
			check_variable = {
				which = "minimal_training_days_active"
				value = 180
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			which = "minimal_training_days_active"
			value = 30
		}
		not = {
			check_variable = {
				which = "minimal_training_days_active"
				value = 180
			}
		}
	}
	land_organisation = -0.05
	air_organisation = -0.05
	naval_organisation = -0.05
	air_intercept = -0.025
	ground_attack = -0.025
	strategic_attack = -0.025
	tactical_attack = -0.025
	org_regain = -0.05
}

AI_WAR_CG = {
	potential = {
		ai = yes
		or = {
			tag = ENG
			tag = CHI
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		war = yes
	}

	dissent = -1.0

	icon = 84
}

SOV_AI_BALANCE = {
	potential = {
		tag = SOV
		ai = yes
		war = yes
	}
	trigger = {}

	#unit_repair = 0.5
	supply_consumption = -0.5
	supply_throughput = 1
	global_manpower_modifier = 4
	#land_organisation = -0.55

	icon = 5
}
SOV_AI_TWEAK = {
	potential = {
		tag = SOV
		ai = yes
	}
	trigger = {
		#GER = {
		#	ai = yes
		#}
		#not = {
		#	year = 1944
		#}
		not = {
			war_with = JAP
		}
		
		or = {
			and = {
				#war_with = GER
				total_amount_of_brigades = 6500
				PER = {
					faction = axis
				}
				TUR = {
					faction = axis
				}
			}
			and = {
				#war_with = GER
				total_amount_of_brigades = 5500
				or = {
					and = {
						PER = {
							faction = axis
						}
						not = {
							TUR = {
								faction = axis
							}
						}
					}
					and = {
						TUR = {
							faction = axis
						}
						not = {
							PER = {
								faction = axis
							}
						}
					}
					and = {
						not = {
							exists = PER
						}
						TUR = {
							faction = axis
						}
					}
				}
			}
			and = {
				#war_with = GER
				total_amount_of_brigades = 5000
				or = {
					not = {
						PER = {
							faction = axis
						}
					}
					not = {
						exists = PER
					}
				}
				not = {
					TUR = {
						faction = axis
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#land_build_speed = 5
	#tank_build_speed = 5
	#air_build_speed = 0.65

	icon = 5
}
SOV_AI_WAR_I = {
	potential = {
		tag = SOV
		ai = yes
	}
	trigger = {
		or = {
			and = {
				#war_with = GER
				not = {
					war_with = JAP
				}
				not = {
					total_amount_of_brigades = 2500
				}
			}
			and = {
				war_with = GER
				war_with = JAP
				not = {
					total_amount_of_brigades = 3000
				}
			}
		}
	}

	land_build_speed = -0.775
	tank_build_speed = -0.775

	icon = 5
}
SOV_AI_WAR_II = {
	potential = {
		tag = SOV
		ai = yes
	}
	trigger = {
		or = {
			and = {
				#war_with = GER
				not = {
					war_with = JAP
				}
				not = {
					total_amount_of_brigades = 3500
				}
				total_amount_of_brigades = 2500
			}
			and = {
				war_with = GER
				war_with = JAP
				not = {
					total_amount_of_brigades = 4500
				}
				total_amount_of_brigades = 3500
			}
		}
	}

	land_build_speed = -0.575
	tank_build_speed = -0.575

	icon = 5
}

Blitz_effect = {
	potential = {
		tag = GER
		2613 = {
			controller = {
				faction = axis
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		has_country_modifier = Paying_for_the_Blitz
	}

	strategic_attack = 0.15
	air_intercept = 0.1
	air_organisation = 0.1

	global_ic = -0.05
	global_money = -0.05
	global_supplies = -0.05

	icon = 7
}

Nat_focus_ground_forces_start = {
	potential = {
		check_variable = {
			which = "ground_forces_national_focus_days_active"
			value = 1
		}
		not = {
			check_variable = {
				which = "ground_forces_national_focus_days_active"
				value = 90
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			which = "ground_forces_national_focus_days_active"
			value = 1
		}
		not = {
			check_variable = {
				which = "ground_forces_national_focus_days_active"
				value = 90
			}
		}
	}

	icon = 5
}

Nat_focus_navy_one = {

###########################################################
###############		 WAR EXHAUSTION 	 	###############
###########################################################

WE_low = {
	potential = {
		check_variable = {
			which = "war_exhaustion"
			value = 1
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			which = "war_exhaustion"
			value = 2500
		}
		not = {
			check_variable = {
				which = "war_exhaustion"
				value = 6500
			}
		}
	}

	ruling_party_support = -0.05
	national_unity = -0.025
	global_manpower_modifier = -0.1

	icon = 5
}
WE_medium = {
	potential = {
		check_variable = {
			which = "war_exhaustion"
			value = 5500
		}
		not = {
			check_variable = {
				which = "war_exhaustion"
				value = 7500
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			which = "war_exhaustion"
			value = 6500
		}
		not = {
			check_variable = {
				which = "war_exhaustion"
				value = 9500
			}
		}
	}

	ruling_party_support = -0.1
	national_unity = -0.05
	global_manpower_modifier = -0.2
	global_revolt_risk = 2

	icon = 5
}
WE_high = {
	potential = {
		check_variable = {
			which = "war_exhaustion"
			value = 8500
		}
		not = {
			check_variable = {
				which = "war_exhaustion"
				value = 11000
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		or = {
			and = {
				war = yes
				check_variable = {
					which = "war_exhaustion"
					value = 9500
				}
				not = {
					check_variable = {
						which = "war_exhaustion"
						value = 11000
					}
				}
			}
			and = {
				war = no
				check_variable = {
					which = "war_exhaustion"
					value = 9500
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ruling_party_support = -0.15
	national_unity = -0.1
	global_manpower_modifier = -0.3
	global_revolt_risk = 4


	icon = 5
}
WE_extreme = {
	potential = {
		war = yes
		check_variable = {
			which = "war_exhaustion"
			value = 9500
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			which = "war_exhaustion"
			value = 11000
		}
	}

	ruling_party_support = -0.25
	national_unity = -0.15
	global_manpower_modifier = -0.45
	global_revolt_risk = 6

	icon = 5
}

###############################################################
###############		event unit IC penalty		###############
###############################################################


### 20% ###
ic_investment_II = {
	potential = {
		ai = no
		check_variable = {
			which = IC_days_spent
			value = 1
		}
		check_variable = {
			which = event_unit_investment
			value = 20
		}
		not = {
			check_variable = {
				which = event_unit_investment
				value = 21
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			which = IC_days_spent
			value = 1
		}
	}

	global_ic = -0.2
}

### Penalty for being 20000 IC days in debt ###
ic_investment_debt_twenty = {
	potential = {
		ai = no
		check_variable = {
			which = IC_days_spent
			value = 10000
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			which = IC_days_spent
			value = 20000
		}
	}
	org_regain = -0.05
	land_organisation = -0.05

### Penalty for being 30000 IC days in debt ###
ic_investment_debt_thirty = {
	potential = {
		ai = no
		check_variable = {
			which = IC_days_spent
			value = 20000
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			which = IC_days_spent
			value = 30000
		}
	}
	org_regain = -0.05
	land_organisation = -0.05
	air_organisation = -0.05
	soft_attack = -0.05
	hard_attack = -0.05
}

		not =  { has_global_flag = NO_MODIFIERS }

			GER = { war_with = SOV }
			not = { year = 1942 }
		}
		tag = HOL
		GER = { has_country_flag = fr_goal_nag_no }
	}

	trigger = {
		war_with = GER
	}

	land_organisation = -0.40
	org_regain = -0.3
	#industrial_efficiency = -0.5
	#global_leadership_modifier = -0.3

	icon = 5
}

					faction = allies
				}
			}
		}
		not = {
			812 = { #Oslo
				controller = {
					faction = allies
				}
			}
		}
		or = {
			not = {
				war_with = ENG
				war_with = FRA
			}
			and = {
				65 = { #Narvik
					controller = {
						faction = axis
					}

					controller = {
						faction = axis
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = german_swedish_agreement
		not = { has_country_flag = german_swedish_agreement_stop }
	}

# Captain of industry
captain_of_industry = {

	potential = {

	}

	trigger = {
		check_variable = { which = aluminium_ActualBalance value = 1001 }
		or = {
			and = {
				check_variable = { which = tank_factory_count value = 20 }
				check_variable = { which = automotive_factory_count value = 20 }
			}
			and = {
				or = {
					check_variable = { which = tank_factory_count value = 25 }
					check_variable = { which = automotive_factory_count value = 25 }
				}
				check_variable = { which = BaseIC value = 500 }
			}
		}

		not = { this = { check_variable = { which = "islandsHopped" value = 9 } } }
		USA = { war_with = JAP	}
	}

			tag = USA
			tag = JAP
		}

lack_of_strat_resource_ship_armor_techs = {

	potential = {
		or = {
			and = {
				Vickers_steel = 1
				not = { check_variable = { which = copper_ActualBalance value = 1000 } }
			}
			and = {
				Cemented_armor  = 1
				not = { check_variable = { which = manganese_ActualBalance value = 1000 } }
				not = { check_variable = { which = chromite_ActualBalance value = 1000 } }
			}
			and = {
				Special_treatment_steel  = 1
				not = { check_variable = { which = nickel_ActualBalance value = 1000 } }
				not = { check_variable = { which = chromite_ActualBalance value = 1000 } }
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = strat_resource_system_normal
		or = {
			and = {
				Vickers_steel = 1
				not = { check_variable = { which = copper_ActualBalance value = 1000 } }
			}
			and = {
				Cemented_armor  = 1
				not = { check_variable = { which = manganese_ActualBalance value = 1000 } }
				not = { check_variable = { which = chromite_ActualBalance value = 1000 } }
			}
			and = {
				Special_treatment_steel  = 1
				not = { check_variable = { which = nickel_ActualBalance value = 1000 } }
				not = { check_variable = { which = chromite_ActualBalance value = 1000 } }
			}
		}
	}

	naval_build_speed = 0.05

	icon = 50
}

				check_variable = { which = nickel_ActualBalance value = 1000 }
				check_variable = { which = chromite_ActualBalance value = 1000 }
			}
		}
	}

		ai = no
		check_variable = {
			which = "BaseIC"
			value = 150
		}
		not = {
			money = 3000
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			which = "BaseIC"
			value = 150
		}
		has_country_flag = budget_over_2000
		not = {
			money = 3000
		}
		date = 1936.7.1
	}

	icon = 41
}
